      if (res.length == 1) {
        total = search;
      } else {
        res.forEach(function (i, idx, array) {
          if (idx === array.length - 1) {
            total += i;
          } else {
            total += i + ",";
          }
        });
      }

      TagManager.ready.then(function () {
        var scriptTag = 'home';
        var typeTag = 'undefined';
        var cookieADB = 'squido-adbd';
        var capaA = 'capa-portada';
        var capaB = 'pop-up';
        var origenTags = 'undefined';

        var results = document.querySelector('.voc-hemeroteca-num-results');
        if (results) {
          if (parseInt(results.textContent) == 0) {
            errorBusqueda = 'cero-resultados';
          }
        }

        var app = Voonto.getInstance();
        var hasCookie = document.cookie.indexOf(cookieADB) > -1;
        var hasTopic = document.referrer.indexOf(typeTag) > -1;
        var promise = Promise.all([
          app.when('blockadblock:ready'),
          app.when('evdab:ready'),
        ]);

              resolvePromiseForCoverContent(promise, hasCookie, capaA, capaB);
        });

      function resolvePromiseForMultimediaContent(promise) {
        promise.then(function () {
          TagManager.set({slot: 1}).track();
        });
      }

      function resolvePromiseForCoverContent(promise, hasCookie, capaA, capaB) {
        promise.then(function ([res1, res2]) {
          if ((res1 || res2) && hasCookie) {
            TagManager.set({capasMostradas: capaA}).track();
          } else if ((res1 || res2) && !hasCookie) {
            TagManager.set({capasMostradas: capaB}).track();
          } else {
            TagManager.track();
          }
        });
      }

      function resolvePromiseForSubCoverContent(promise, hasCookie, capaA, capaB) {
        promise.then(function ([res1, res2]) {
          if ((res1 || res2) && hasCookie) {
            TagManager.set({capasMostradas: capaA}).track();
          }
          if ((res1 || res2) && !hasCookie) {
            TagManager.set({capasMostradas: capaB}).track();
          }
        });
      }

      function resolvePromiseForNewsContent(promise, hasTopic, capaA, origenTags) {
        promise.then(function ([res1, res2]) {
          if (res1 || res2 && hasTopic) {
            TagManager.set({capasMostradas: capaA, origenTags: origenTags}).track();
          } else if (res1 || res2 && !hasTopic) {
            TagManager.set({capasMostradas: capaA}).track();
          } else if (hasTopic) {
            TagManager.set({origenTags: origenTags}).track();
          } else {
            TagManager.track();
          }
        });
      }

      function resolvePromiseForMediaContent(promise, capaA) {
        promise.then(function ([res1, res2]) {
          if (res1 || res2) {
            TagManager.set({capasMostradas: capaA, slot: 1}).track();
          } else {
            TagManager.set({slot: 1}).track();
          }
        });
      }

      function resolvePromiseForArchiveResultContent(promise, hasCookie, capaA, total, errorBusqueda) {
        promise.then(function ([res1, res2]) {
          if ((res1 || res2) && hasCookie) {
            TagManager.set({
              capasMostradas: capaA,
              keyword: total,
              tipoBuscador: 'hemeroteca',
              errorBusqueda: errorBusqueda
            }).track();
          } else if ((res1 || res2) && !hasCookie) {
            TagManager.set({
              capasMostradas: capaB,
              keyword: total,
              tipoBuscador: 'hemeroteca',
              errorBusqueda: errorBusqueda
            }).track();
          } else {
            TagManager.set({
              keyword: total,
              tipoBuscador: 'hemeroteca',
              errorBusqueda: errorBusqueda
            }).track();
          }
        });
      }
  </script>

           var campaign = [];
        var i = 0;
                            campaign[i]=[];
            campaign[i] = {'campaign':'default','logo':'https://oferplan.laverdad.es/static/images/logos/lv/oferplan_logo.svg','bgcolor':'#03a9f4'};
            i++;
                            campaign[i]=[];
            campaign[i] = {'campaign':'gastroplan','logo':'https://oferplan.laverdad.es/static/images/logos/lv/gastroplan_logo.svg','bgcolor':'#C0A052'};
            i++;
                            campaign[i]=[];
            campaign[i] = {'campaign':'murciaentradas','logo':'https://oferplan.laverdad.es/static/images/logos/lv/murciaentradas_logo.svg','bgcolor':'#E2BE27'};
            i++;
                            campaign[i]=[];
            campaign[i] = {'campaign':'navidad','logo':'https://oferplan.laverdad.es/static/images/logos/lv/oferplan_logo.svg','bgcolor':'#03A9F4'};
            i++;
                            campaign[i]=[];
            campaign[i] = {'campaign':'despensa','logo':'https://oferplan.laverdad.es/static/images/logos/lv/gastroplan_logo.svg','bgcolor':'#C0A052'};
            i++;
                            campaign[i]=[];
            campaign[i] = {'campaign':'amercook','logo':'https://oferplan.laverdad.es/static/images/logos/lv/oferplan_logo.svg','bgcolor':'#7BB392'};
            i++;
                var slug = 'lv';
        var url = 'https://oferplan.laverdad.es/';
        var moduleFuncs = function() {
            var medio = document.getElementById("oferplan-header").dataset['slug'];

            var pathname = window.location.pathname;
            var utm_content = 'portada';
            if(pathname !== '/'){
                var splited_paths = pathname.split('/');
                if(splited_paths[splited_paths.length-1] === ''){
                    // subdomain. remove empty spaces
                    splited_paths = splited_paths.filter(function(v){return v!==''});
                    utm_content = splited_paths.join('-');
                }else{
                    // subdomain with file ending
                    splited_paths.pop();
                    splited_paths = splited_paths.filter(function(v){return v!==''});
                    utm_content = splited_paths.join('-');
                }
            }

            var nssource = window.location.hostname;
            var cromos = document.getElementById('voc-oferplan').querySelectorAll('.swiper-container a, .oferplan-header a');
            for(var i = 0; i < cromos.length; i++) {
                var item = cromos[i];
                var href = item.getAttribute('href');
                if (typeof href !== 'undefined') {
                    href = href.replace(/xxmarketingcontentxx/g, utm_content.toLowerCase());
                    href = href.replace(/xxnssourcexx/g, nssource.toLowerCase());
                    item.setAttribute('href', href);
                }
            }
            var el = document.querySelector('[data-voc-carousel-oferplan]'); // se obtiene el elemento que contiene el listener
            href = document.getElementById('voc-oferplan').getElementsByClassName("swiper-slide")[0].firstElementChild.href;
            document.getElementById('oferplan-header').setAttribute("href", href);
            el.swiper.on('slideChangeStart', function() {
                for(var i = 0; i < campaign.length; i++){
                    if (document.getElementById('voc-oferplan').getElementsByClassName('swiper-slide-active')[0].classList.contains(campaign[i]['campaign'])) {
                        document.getElementById('oferplan-header').style  =  'background-color: #eff0f1 !important;  background-image:url("'+campaign[i]["logo"]+'") !important;';
                        document.getElementById('voc-oferplan').style = 'background: linear-gradient(180deg,'+campaign[i]['bgcolor']+' 0,'+campaign[i]["bgcolor"]+' 57%,#eff0f1 0,#eff0f1) !important;';
                        break;
                    }else{
                        document.getElementById('oferplan-header').style = "";
                        document.getElementById('voc-oferplan').style = 'background: linear-gradient(180deg,#d6cd2e 0,#d6cd2e 57%,#eff0f1 0,#eff0f1) !important;';
                    }
                }
                href = document.getElementById('voc-oferplan').getElementsByClassName("swiper-slide-active")[0].firstElementChild.href;
                document.getElementById('oferplan-header').setAttribute("href", href);
            });
        };
        Voonto.ready.then(function(app){
            app.on('swiper:ready', function(){
                moduleFuncs();
            });
        });
